==================== 测试诊断索引 ====================
test diagnostics index:
- quick start: open logs/summary.txt first, then logs/recent-errors.txt, then logs/by-trace.txt.
- protocol frames: search PROTOCOL_TX / PROTOCOL_RX, M90RealSerial, M90StubSerial, DvrSerialMonitor, DvrSerialDispatchUseCase, GpsSerialMonitor, Jt808SocketMonitor, LegacyStationDisplay, JhyPassengerCounterMonitor.
- station flow: search StationBusinessModule, station-action, gps-auto-report, station-snapshot, LegacyStationDisplay.
- dispatch/network flow: search DispatchBusinessModule, JT808, AL808, sendProfessionRequest, socket/monitor-status.txt, device/dumpsys-connectivity.txt.
- audio playback: audio is not a protocol frame; search LegacyStationAudio, station-audio-plan, station-audio-player, station-audio-player-error, station-audio-gpio, station-audio-volume, station-audio-tts; also read device/dumpsys-audio.txt and device/dumpsys-media-session.txt.
- DVR/video/touch: search LegacyMainActivity, home-monitor, home-dvr-touch, DvrSerialMonitor, DvrSerialDispatchUseCase, dvr raw, DVR 在线, DVR 离线, CameraAdapter; also read logs/android-logcat-warnings.txt.
- GPIO/device operations: search DEVICE, GPIO, writePin, TerminalSelfCheck, device/self-check.txt.
- CAN state: current code has CAN config/self-check only, no CAN business tx/rx adapter yet; read CAN 检查, can-link-state, can-proc-stats, can-proc-receive-list.
- GPS/resources: search GpsSerialMonitor, gps raw sample, gps-fix, GpsBusinessModule, LegacyGpsAutoReportEngine, gps-auto-report, JT808 路口, 路口超速, StationResourceArchiveUseCase, config/raw-terminal-config.json.
- RFID/sign-in: search RFID, SignInBusinessModule, read_card, manual_sign_out, dispatch attendance.
- file/import/export/OSS: search FileBusinessModule, StationResourceArchiveUseCase, OssDebugBundleUploader, export_bundle, import_station_resources.
- upgrade/download: search LegacyUpgradeDownloadAgent, HTTP 下载, FTP 下载, 8B0A, endpoint.
- system state: read config/*, modules/module-status.txt, device/foundation-status.txt, device/system-properties.txt, device/dumpsys-package.txt, device/df.txt.
- known blind spots: DVR firmware private logs, kernel logs blocked by permission, and purely visual/audio physical effects still need photo/video or on-site measurement.

==================== 日志覆盖说明 ====================
log coverage map:
- protocol tx/rx: logs/app-log.txt, logs/by-module.txt, logs/by-trace.txt; categories PROTOCOL_TX / PROTOCOL_RX include SerialPortAdapter tx/rx, socket, DVR, GPS NMEA, JHY, station-display, JT808/AL808, crossing and overspeed frames.
- business flow: category BIZ includes station, dispatch, sign-in, upgrade/download, GPS auto-report, passenger counter, file import/export decisions.
- ui flow: category UI includes legacy home actions, DVR touch coordinates, monitor mode changes, setup/file/login page actions.
- device operations: category DEVICE includes GPIO, camera, RFID, serial/socket open-close, system reboot/install/time operations.
- failures: logs/recent-errors.txt plus category ERROR entries in app-log/by-module/by-trace.
- runtime state: config/*, device/*, gps/monitor-status.txt, socket/monitor-status.txt, modules/module-status.txt.
- android system snapshot: logs/android-logcat*.txt, device/system-properties.txt, device/dumpsys-*.txt, device/can-*.txt, device/df.txt, device/mount.txt.
- test phase policy: verbose evidence first; reduce log volume only after the related function passes testing.
- external evidence still needed for DVR internal firmware logs, kernel logs blocked by Android permissions, and visual/audio-only effects.

==================== 配置摘要 ====================
当前配置: M90-STUB / 版本 2026.04.13 / 来源 runtime:/storage/emulated/0/Android/data/com.lhxy.istationdevice.android11/files/config/terminal-config.runtime.json
串口:
- rs232_1 -> ttyS3 @9600 [stub]
- rs232_2 -> ttyS4 @9600 [stub]
- gps -> ttyS5 @115200 [stub]
- rs485_1 -> ttyS7 @38400 [stub]
- rs485_2 -> ttyS9 @9600 [stub]
Socket:
- jt808 -> 211.154.159.34:7000 [stub]
- al808 -> 211.154.159.34:7000 [stub]
GPIO: [stub]
- inner_audio -> GPIO1_B1
- outer_audio -> GPIO1_B2
- inner_speaker -> GPIO0_D6
- io1 -> GPIO1_D0
- io2 -> GPIO1_D1
- io5 -> GPIO1_D4
Camera: [stub]
- av_out -> cameraId 100
- reverse -> cameraId 101
- middle_door -> cameraId 102
- monitor -> cameraId 103
RFID: [stub] / 命令=- / 文件=- / I2C=-@0x00
SystemOps: [stub] / 静默安装=false / 重启=false / 校时=false
Location: [stub] / enabled=false / provider=gps
CAN: [stub]
Keyboard: [stub] / serial=keyboard / protocol=serial
回放入口:
- 屏显走 rs485_1
- GPS 走 gps
- JT808 走 jt808
- AL808 走 al808
- 默认 GPIO 走 inner_audio
- 视频监视 GPIO-A 走 io1
- 视频监视 GPIO-B 走 io2
- 默认 Camera 走 av_out
系统设置:
- 报站: 内音=12 / 外音=12 / 属性=up_down / 外音开关=true
- 资源: 导入=true / 线路=5 / 方向=上行 / 属性=对开 / 来源=line-choice
- TTS: 开关=true / 内音=8 / 外音=8
- 语言=auto
- 其他: 喊话=50 / 调度=7 / 车号=- / 喊话GPIO-A=- / 喊话GPIO-B=-
- 协议互斥: dispatchOwner=serial_rs232_1
